{Embed}
tux-linux
https://github.com/Kobo-InkBox/inkbox/issues/47#issuecomment-1518854982
[Kobo-InkBox/inkbox] New comment on issue #47: Kobo Nia: diagnostics mode on installation
> @tux-linux how is it even possible? Nia doesn't have a second button to enter this mode during boot?

You can enter this mode by pressing the power button repeatedly or just holding it in this case. The BDK is for other devices which have a secondary button. This boots a basic GUI using FBInk with serial-only user interaction to perform first-necessity recovery operations.
This particular recovery mode is made with Qt components and allows for a broader range of recovery operations, and ...

Szybet
https://github.com/Kobo-InkBox/inkbox/discussions/52#discussioncomment-6284537
[Kobo-InkBox/inkbox] New comment on discussion #52: Actual "user" documentation?
1. connect the ereader to the pc
2. click OK on the dialog that appeared
3. upload your books
4. unmount the ereader
5. unplug the cable
6. wait
7. that's it :D

Power the device off, turn it on and spam clicking the power button, then in diagnostics mode root the device - then ssh, usbnet can be enabled and you can access the rootfs ( well in your example, if you can, the serial connection will be the easiest to use )

[Kobo-InkBox/inkbox] New comment on issue #63: Building Instructions
if you encounter init building problems, add:
```
INIT_GCC="/home/build/inkbox/kernel/toolchain/armv7l-linux-musleabihf-cross/bin/armv7l-linux-musleabihf-gcc" INIT_STRIP="/home/build/inkbox/kernel/toolchain/armv7l-linux-musleabihf-cross/bin/armv7l-linux-musleabihf-strip"
```

it's basically removing rootfs cache at each boot, and it forces mounting it read-only even if RW_ROOTFS flag is set to true
(only for std kernel)

[inkbox] New discussion #65: r/explainlikei'mfive Why cant I run InkBox on a tablet that are not officially supported?
Hello! I know this is a pretty dumb question, but i have virtually no experience with operating systems and what they require. My main goal for this question is to possibly get a quick rundown of what this OS needs to run on my own tablet, or any other tablet that isn't supported, as I'm willing to learn and possibly help develop it for other tablets. 

I have a boox max lumi 2, and if you aren't aware [they have broken the gpl license](http://bbs.onyx-international.com/t/install-linux-or-a...

tux-linux
https://github.com/Kobo-InkBox/inkbox/discussions/65#discussioncomment-8203364
[Kobo-InkBox/inkbox] New comment on discussion #65: r/explainlikei'mfive Why cant I run InkBox on a e-ink tablet thats not officially supported?
Hello!

Yes, I am aware that Boox is violating the GPL license for their Linux/Android kernels, which makes it virtually impossible to do anything with them unless you're willing to get into a LOT of reverse-engineering, a thing which I don't even ever want to think about doing. To give you an idea, you would probably have to figure out:
- how the RAM chip is working (although this might partly be the bootloader's job, which sources I suspect are not available either)
- how the CPU works ...

[inkbox] Discussion #65 marked answered: r/explainlikei'mfive Why cant I run InkBox on a e-ink tablet thats not officially supported?
Hello!

Yes, I am aware that Boox is violating the GPL license for their Linux/Android kernels, which makes it virtually impossible to do anything with them unless you're willing to get into a LOT of reverse-engineering, a thing which I don't even ever want to think about doing. To give you an idea, you would probably have to figure out:
- how the RAM chip is working (although this might partly be the bootloader's job, which sources I suspect are not available either)
- how the CPU works ...

tux-linux
https://github.com/Kobo-InkBox/inkbox/issues/67#issuecomment-1939678478
[Kobo-InkBox/inkbox] New comment on issue #67: Kobo Glo HD N437 - No browser?
On-screen boot also works for non-root devices. You can enable it by writing true to [p1]/flags/BOOT_USB_DEBUG
P1 is preferably mountable with Linux (ext4)

[Kobo-InkBox/inkbox] New comment on issue #70: Gutenberg Integration Improvements
Hi, these are good ideas, but unfortunately probably very hard to implement as we rely solely on regular expressions to parse Gutenberg catalog. You can have a look here and see for yourself:
https://github.com/Kobo-InkBox/rootfs/tree/master/usr/local/bin/gutenberg
As far as I can see, the csv catalog does not provide information for most popular books.
